DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `conf_city`;

  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx1` (`state`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=3573 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
